# PetAmzStore

> PetAmzStore (petamzstore.com) is a US-based online pet supplies retailer 
> offering a curated selection of premium products for dogs and cats.

## About

PetAmzStore is dedicated to helping pet owners find high-quality, 
health-focused products for their furry companions. The store ships 
across the United States and is built on Shopify.

## Product Categories

- **Dental Treats & Chews** — Fish-shaped and antler-shaped dental treats 
  (Trophy Chews™), and breed-specific soft chews for hunting dogs (Breedwise).
- **Health Supplements** — Mobility Bites and Calming Bites for dogs, 
  available in 100-count jars.
- **Pet Accessories** — Cooling bandanas and themed bandanas for dogs.
- **Waste Management** — Eco-friendly dog waste bags and leash dispensers 
  by beyondGREEN, made in the USA.
- **Natural Treats** — Single-ingredient dehydrated beef liver treats 
  for cats and dogs.

## Key Details

- **Domain:** petamzstore.com
- **Currency:** USD
- **Location:** United States
- **Fulfillment:** Dropshipping via Zendrop and third-party logistics (3PL)
- **Sales Channels:** Online store, Instagram Shopping

## Usage Notes

This store sells pet health, nutrition, and lifestyle products. 
Content on this site is intended for pet owners seeking quality 
supplies for their dogs and cats. Product descriptions, pricing, 
and availability are subject to change.

Whether you add it to kibble, layer with a soft treat on a lick mat, or mix into wet food, this ground version of our Fish Chips single-ingredient treats just might be your new "o-fish-al" go-to healthy pet food topper! HUMAN-GRADE FISH: A HEALTHY FOOD TOPPER FOR DOGS AND CATS Dogs and cats alike love the "umami" flavor of fresh fish. With our fish pet food topper, they can enjoy it at any meal or snack time! Made with 100% human-grade walleye fillets - and no byproducts, additives or offal - Fish Treat Topper provides nothing but lean protein, essential amino acids and vital nutrients with every serving. Plus, this unique powdered version of our Fish Chips healthy pet treats lacks the strong fishy smell of other fish-based pet foods, making it popular with the humans serving it, too! SUSTAINABLE SINGLE-INGREDIENT PET SNACK Like all Farm to Pet products, our Fish Treat Topper contains just one ingredient - in this case, human-grade walleye fish fillets. Not only is it a delicious source of complete protein for cats and dogs, it is also easy to digest and low in allergens, especially important for pets with food sensitivities or chicken allergies. What's more, the walleye is sustainably fished from Lake Erie according to the 100% Great Lakes Fish Initiative for minimal environmental disruption with maximum pet nutrition. PAW-FECT FOR PROTEIN ROTATION Getting enough animal protein is critical to pet health and wellness. Rotating those proteins gives even finicky pets flavor and variety as it helps ensure a more complete spectrum of nutrients and amino acids. For instance, poultry is a good source of niacin and taurine, beef provides healthy doses of iron and choline, and walleye is rich in astaxanthin and vitamin A. Plus, Farm to Pet food toppers contain 2-3 times more protein than other dog food toppers on the market! So many ways for dogs and cats to get so much pet nutrition! HOW TO USE POWDER DOG FOOD TOPPERS Incorporating food toppers into your pet's daily diet is a cinch with Farm to Pet Treat Toppers! Thanks to a break-resistant jar and a convenient shake-or-spoon top, it's easy to sprinkle this protein powder for pets over wet food or dry kibble, pour on top of a lick mat recipe, or mix into broths, homemade pet treats and even medicines. Fish Treat Topper is also a great food topper for senior dogs and puppies who may need higher protein intake. No matter how you choose to use our healthy pet food toppers, fur babies get an instant boost of flavor and nutrition every time! WHY CHOOSE FARM TO PET FISH DOG FOOD TOPPER Farm to Pet's one-of-a-kind fish pet food topper makes it easy to add the flavor and nutrition of human-grade walleye to pet foods, snacks and lick mats. This lean source of complete protein is rich in many nutrients that support overall pet health, including essential amino acids, minerals and antioxidants. Plus, making healthy pet food toppers out of our single-ingredient protein chips reduces waste as it provides more ways for dogs and cats to enjoy nutritious pet treats! FARM TO PET DOG FOOD TOPPER FEEDING GUIDELINES Base serving size on your pet's size and appetite. Start with a sprinkle and go up from there to supplement protein and nutrients in your pet’s diet. Pets 15 pounds or less can have up to 2-5 teaspoons of this low-calorie food topper per day; pets 16-35 pounds, up to 5-7 teaspoons; and large dogs, up to 8 teaspoons. Check with your veterinarian for specific guidance for your dog, especially if he has any specific dietary needs or restrictions. HOW TO USE FISH DOG FOOD TOPPER Here are just a few of the ways your dog or cat can enjoy our healthy single-ingredient Treat Toppers pet food toppers: Sprinkle onto kibble or wet food. Mix with  or broth. Pour into licking mats. Use in DIY healthy pet treat recipes. FISH DOG FOOD TOPPER FAQS WHAT IS A DOG FOOD TOPPER? Dog food toppers are designed to be added to a pet’s regular food to enhance flavor and/or nutritional value. Meal toppers for dogs and cats are not meant to be substitutes for pet food but rather to supplement pet diets. Pet food toppers are available in various forms, including bone broths, purees, bits, or powders. Meal toppers like our powdered single-ingredient dog food toppers offer a simple way to make meals more appealing and easier to eat; support overall pet health; cater to specific needs or dental issues; increase dietary protein or omega-3 fatty acids; or add variety to a pet’s diet. WHY ARE SINGLE-INGREDIENT DOG FOOD TOPPERS BETTER? Single-ingredient food toppers for dogs are easier on pet digestive systems than dog food toppers with multiple ingredients, especially those that are highly processed. Our low-allergen fish dog food topper powder is an easy to digest meal topper for dogs and cats, made from sustainably-fished human-grade walleye fish fillets gently dehydrated to provide the nutrients and complete protein pets need to thrive with natural flavor they love. WHAT MAKES FARM TO PET DOG FOOD TOPPERS SPECIAL? Unlike other dog food toppers that contain byproducts, meals and offal, Farm to Pet fish dog food topper contains only human-grade walleye fillets with no skin or bones. We offer our US-made dog food toppers in chicken, turkey, beef, fish and antler powder varieties, making them ideal for protein rotation and to provide a full spectrum of amino acids and high levels of minerals with low levels of fat and cholesterol. A powdered version of our Fish Chips for dogs, our low-odor fish dog food topper is a great meal supplement for dogs with sensitive stomachs, food topper for overweight dogs, meal topper for picky eaters, food topper for senior dogs, and of course for pets with chicken allergies. WHY SHOULD I USE A DOG FOOD TOPPER? Using a dog food topper can make mealtime more exciting and nutritious for your furry friend. A topper like Farm to Pet Fish Dog Food Topper adds flavor, encouraging picky eaters to enjoy their meals, while also boosting protein, vitamins, and minerals that support overall health. It’s an easy way to enhance your dog’s diet without overhauling their regular food, making every meal both tasty and wholesome. Dog food toppers are also great for dogs with missing or broken teeth or to use as a healthy lickable pet treat on lick mats or in DIY dog treat recipes. CAN CATS EAT DOG FOOD TOPPERS? Both dogs and cats are carnivores, so they both love and need animal protein like poultry, beef and fish. Like dogs of any age and size, cats can safely enjoy Farm to Pet dog food toppers. Cats also love our Crumbles cat treats, made from the same dehydrated human-grade proteins in small morsels ideal for smaller mouths! HOW MUCH DOG FOOD TOPPER SHOULD I GIVE MY PET? As a rule, pets can usually enjoy 10-20 percent of their daily calories in pet treats including pet food toppers. Even though many of us don’t know what our pet’s daily calorie target is or how many calories they take in, you can base the amount of food topper to give your dog or cat on their weight and appetite. Our grain-free fish dog food topper has just 3 calories per teaspoon. This means your small pet (under 15 pounds) can have up to 3-5 teaspoons per day; medium pets (15-35 pounds), 4-6 teaspoons; and large dogs (over 35 pounds), up to 8-10 teaspoons. Ask your vet for confirmation or if you’re looking for guidance about food toppers for diabetic dogs or cats, toppers for pets on a diet, meal toppers for puppies or kittens, or other special circumstances.

For overzealous pups, feed in your open palm to avoid accidental finger nipping! CHICKEN DOG TREAT FAQS WHY ARE SINGLE INGREDIENT TREATS GOOD FOR DOGS? Single-ingredient treats for dogs are easier on canine digestive systems than dog treats with multiple ingredients, especially if they are highly processed. Our highly digestible chicken dog treats are simply the best chicken treats for dogs, made from hormone-free human-grade chicken breast meat, gently dehydrated to provide the nutrients and complete protein dogs need to thrive and natural flavor they love. WHAT MAKES FARM TO PET CHICKEN DOG TREATS SPECIAL? Unlike other dog treats that contain byproducts, meals and fillers, Farm to Pet chicken dog treats contain only human-grade chicken breast that’s boneless, skinless and sourced from local farms. Our US made chicken dog treats are an excellent way to rotate proteins for dogs, offering a full spectrum of amino acids and high levels of potassium with low levels of fat and cholesterol. This makes our grain-free chicken chips a great dog treat option for overweight dogs, treats for diabetic dogs, and treats for training dogs. Break them into pieces to create small bite size chicken treats for puppies and treats for small dogs. HOW MANY DOG TREATS CAN MY DOG HAVE IN A DAY? As a rule, dogs can usually enjoy 10-20 percent of their daily calories in treats. However, many of us don’t know what our dog’s daily calorie target is or how many calories they take in! Luckily, you can base how many treats to give your dog on your dog’s size. Our grain-free chicken dog treats have 7 calories per chip. This means your small pup can have from 2-4 chicken chips for dogs per day; medium dogs can eat 5-7 chips, and large dogs can enjoy up to 10 chips per day. Our Chicken Crumbles are a rich source of protein, essential amino acids, B vitamins, and minerals, all with just 3 calories per tablespoon-sized serving and less than 3% fat. Luckily, cats love the delicious flavor of farm-fresh human-grade chicken breast in these nutritious snacks for pets just as much! WHY CHOOSE FARM TO PET CHICKEN CRUMBLES HEALTHY CAT TREATS When it comes to the best healthy pet treats, Farm to Pet has you covered! Our single-ingredient Chicken Crumbles are the perfect healthy snack for cats, gently crafted from all-natural human-grade chicken breast and nothing else. Made in the USA, these natural grain-free cat treats combine the pure poultry taste cats love with the low-fat protein-rich nutrition pet parents seek in every crunchy morsel. Is Maisy meowing for variety? Try our Turkey Crumbles, Fish Crumbles, and Beef Crumbles cat treats, too! CHICKEN CAT TREAT  ANALYSIS Crude Protein (min)......80%Crude Fat (min)..............3%Crude Fiber (max)...........1%Moisture (max)..............10% Each tablespoon of chicken cat treats has 3 calories. CHICKEN CAT TREAT TREAT INGREDIENT SOURCE Farmed in the Midwestern USA FARM TO PET CAT TREAT FEEDING GUIDELINES Base daily cat treat servings on your cat’s size. Feed your small cat (up to 7 pounds) 3-5 tablespoons of Crumbles cat treats, your medium cat (7-12 pounds) 4-6 tablespoons, or your larger cat up to 7 tablespoons per day. Check with your veterinarian for specific guidance for your cat, especially if there are any specific dietary needs or restrictions. HOW TO USE CHICKEN CAT TREATS Here are a few ways to serve our grain-free healthy cat treats: Feed Crumbles by hand for purr-fect cat-human bonding time. Pour into a bowl or plate for independent feline snacking. Add to wet food for a crunchy surprise. CHICKEN CAT TREAT FAQS ARE SINGLE INGREDIENT TREATS GOOD FOR CATS? Since they are easier on feline digestive systems than cat treats with multiple ingredients, single-ingredient treats are excellent for cats, especially if they are minimally processed like Farm to Pet cat treats. Our highly digestible chicken cat treats are simply the best chicken treats for cats, made from human-grade hormone-free chicken breast, gently dehydrated to provide the nutrients and complete protein cats need to thrive and natural poultry flavor they love. WHY ARE HIGH PROTEIN TREATS BETTER FOR CATS? While dogs and cats are both carnivores who thrive on animal protein, cats are actually “obligate carnivores.” This means that they literally cannot survive unless they get the full spectrum of amino acids present in animal proteins like meat, poultry and fish from their diets. Cat treats that are rich in protein help cats get their daily requirements of this macronutrient rather than filling up on other calorie sources like carbohydrates and fat already present in most cat food. Our pure-protein pet food toppers are another great source of complete protein for cats! WHAT MAKES FARM TO PET CHICKEN CAT TREATS SPECIAL? Unlike other cat treats that contain byproducts, meals and fillers, Farm to Pet chicken cat treats contain only human-grade chicken breast - boneless, skinless and locally farmed. Our US-made cat treats are an excellent way to rotate proteins for cats, offering a full spectrum of amino acids and essential vitamins and minerals with low levels of fat and calories. This makes our grain-free chicken treats a great treat option for overweight cats, cat treats for diabetic cats, and even small bite size chicken treats for puppies and treats for small dogs. HOW MANY CAT TREATS CAN MY CAT HAVE IN A DAY? As a rule, cats can usually enjoy 10-20 percent of their daily calories in treats. However, many of us don’t know what our cat’s daily calorie target is or how many calories they take in! Luckily, you can base how many treats to give your cat on your cat’s size. Our pure chicken cat treats have just 3 calories per tablespoon. We suggest 3-5 tablespoons of Crumbles cat treats per day for small cats (up to 7 pounds); 4-6 tablespoons per day for your medium cat (7-12 pounds), and up to 7 tablespoons for your large cat (13+ pounds). Ask your vet for confirmation or if you’re looking for guidance about treats for diabetic cats, treats for overweight cats, treats for kittens, or other special circumstances. CAN DOGS EAT CHICKEN CAT TREATS? Both cats and dogs are carnivores, so they both love and need animal protein like fish, poultry, and beef. Like cats of any age and size, dogs can safely enjoy Farm to Pet cat treats. However, better yet, check out our selection of healthy dog treats, made from the same dehydrated human-grade proteins in crunchable dog-friendly chips!

As opposed to licking paws, shoes or you, lick mats for dogs and cats offer enrichment, distraction and calming effects - especially ideal during grooming visits or bath time. By working diligently to get foods and treats out of the grooves, pets enjoy a satisfying challenge and mental stimulation as well as a tasty reward. Use the back of a spoon to press into the grooves of the licking mat. Use the suction cups to affix the mat to a smooth surface and voila! A soothing nutritious dog treat "sundae" furry friends love! Licking also stimulates saliva production which helps promote fresh breath, healthy teeth and gums, and proper digestion. Provides an outlet for energy and the urge to lick. Stimulates saliva to aid digestion. Helps avoid overfeeding. A healthy way to feed pets nutritious treats and snacks. HOW TO USE A DOG LICK MAT Spread or pour a soft treat like peanut butter, cream cheese or yogurt on the surface of the lick mat Top with a meal topper or pet food supplement like antler powder if desired. Press gently into the grooves of the licking mat. When finished, rinse excess treat from the mat and wash by hand in warm soapy water or on the top rack of the dishwasher. DOG LICK MAT RECIPE IDEAS Here are just a few treats your dog can enjoy on a lick mat using Farm to Pet’s US-made single-ingredient protein-rich pet food toppers: Top a base of natural creamy peanut butter with chicken dog food topper. Try unseasoned plain mashed potatoes with beef dog food topper. Layer cream cheese with Farm to Pet fish pet food topper. Spread unseasoned plain sweet potato mash onto lick mat and top with turkey dog food topper. Add antler powder pet food supplement to a base of plain yogurt mixed with pumpkin puree. Come up with your own dog lick mat recipes based on your dog's needs and preferences! Consult your vet for a complete list of foods that are suitable for your pet. DOG LICK MAT FAQS WHAT IS A LICKING MAT AND HOW DOES IT WORK? A licking mat is a textured surface designed to hold soft pet treats or pet foods. As your dog or cat licks the mat, it provides mental stimulation, slows down eating, and helps soothe anxiety by releasing endorphins. WHAT CAN I PUT ON A LICKING MAT? You can use natural spreadable pet-friendly treats like natural peanut butter (xylitol-free), plain yogurt, pumpkin puree, wet food, unsweetened baby food, mashed fruits or veggies. Always make sure foods and ingredients are pet-safe, and consult your vet with any concerns. HOW DO I CLEAN MY LICK MAT? Sodapup licking mats are dishwasher-safe (top rack only). For handwashing, soak in warm, soapy water and use a brush to remove food residue. ARE LICKING MATS SAFE FOR DOGS AND CATS? Yes, both cats and dogs have a natural urge to lick. It may take a few times before your pet takes to a licking mat. Be sure to always supervise pets while using lick mats or any pet enrichment toy. Some pets may try to chew the mat; remove it if they start biting instead of licking or if the mat becomes damaged. CAN I PUT MY LICKING MAT IN THE FREEZER? These lick mats are freezer safe. Freezing extends the time it will take your pet to finish the treat and offers pets a different treat experience. Spread your pet’s favorite food on the lick mat, freeze it for 1-2 hours, and serve. This makes a great cool treat on a hot day. HOW DO I CHOOSE THE RIGHT LICK MAT FOR MY PET? Choose based on your pet’s size, licking style and propensity, and preferred texture. Soft silicone mats with shallow grooves are great for beginners and casual lickers, while tougher mats with deeper patterns suit stronger lickers and tongues. Licking mats with suction cups are great for car rides, bath time, or any time you need extra assurance the mat will stay put while in use.

ReNewedPet® Ear Cleaning Drops: This all-natural pet ear cleaning drops are made with organic ingredients to remove, and dry, wax build-up and debris in your pet's ears. ReNewedPet® Ear Drops are formulated to reduce this chronic debris build-up, rather than just remove it for it to only redeposit a few days later as with other products.DIRECTIONS FOR USE:PRIMARY PHASE: To reduce over-all build-up, insert as many drops as needed to fill your pet's ear canal with the ear cleaning liquid daily. The daily  must be continued for a period of no less than 7 days, depending on the severity of the build-up in your pet's ears. (Be cautious to watch your pet's ears closely during the  as we have found some pet's will have some slight irritation around day 5-7, so use your judgment and discontinue daily drops if needed.) Do not clean your pets ears out during the primary phase, simply insert the drops daily. Only clean the area outside of the ear canal as the product begins to pull the debris clear of the inner ear. After the primary phase, clean your pet’s ears thoroughly using a cotton pad or cotton swab wet with product; (NEVER USE A Q-TIP IN YOUR PETS EARS!) Check your pet's ears again in 3 days, if all debris is still gone you can continue with the maintenance phase. If after 3 days more debris has built up, you will need to continue with daily application for an additional week, and then recheck. Pricing: Regular: $19 • Extra Large: $25 Crafted from decommissioned 1.75" polyester fire hose, these rugged dog toys are built for dogs who play hard. The hoses used are new and unused—they’ve never been through a fire. Some were taken out of  due to minor defects like leaks, making them unsuitable for firefighting but perfect for repurposing into something your dog will love. Each toy is handmade in the USA and reinforced with mil-spec 1" binding and stitched ends, creating a tough, durable toy designed for fetching and playing. Important Note: These are new hoses that have never been exposed to fire or harsh chemicals. Due to the reclaimed nature of the material, colors, markings, and patterns will vary, and may not exactly match product photos. That’s part of what makes each toy one-of-a-kind. Available Sizes: Regular: Approx. 12” long × 3” wide (laying flat) Extra Large: Approx. 15” long × 4” wide (laying flat) Made in America — Supports First Responders By purchasing this toy, you’re helping reduce waste, support sustainable repurposing, and honor the service of firefighters by giving retired gear new life. Important Usage Notice This toy is built for fetch and supervised play — not for chewing.While the fire hose body is extremely tough, any dog left unattended can eventually chew through the hose itself, including the mil-spec binding and stitched ends. This is normal dog behavior and not a product defect. For best results: Use as a fetch or tug toy only Do not leave your dog alone with the toy Remove immediately if damaged Durable, but not indestructible.Supervision is required for safe use.

- [Live Organic Superworms](https://petamzstore.com/products/live-organic-superworms): Superworms are a highly nutritious meal for pets. They are high in calories, fats, and protein, and they provide a good amount of hydration. For bearded dragons, it is recommended to feed 1-2 super worms per week, or in moderation due to their high fat content. However, they can be given to malnourished or recovering bearded dragons more frequently to help them gain weight. It is not recommended to feed Superworms to very young or baby bearded dragons, as the thicker chitin can lead to impaction. We have 2 sizes: Small - Under 1.25 inches long, these are younger worms. Large - Over 1.25 inches long, these are our older more mature worms.

- [4-ALL PETS EAR, NAIL & EYEWASH KIT](https://petamzstore.com/products/4-all-pets-ear-nail-eyewash-kit): ReNewedPet® grooming and health products are Holistic Vet , and each made with only 100% natural, non-gmo, and organic ingredients. ReNewedPet® Ear Cleaning Drops: This all-natural pet ear cleaning drops are made with organic ingredients to remove, and dry, wax build-up and debris in your pet's ears. Most often, ear debris is caused by a chronic yeast infection in pet's which commonly goes un-diagnosed and untreated by veterinarians. ReNewedPet® Ear Drops are formulated to reduce this chronic debris build-up, rather than just remove it for it to only redeposit a few days later as with other products.DIRECTIONS FOR USE:PRIMARY PHASE: To reduce over-all build-up, insert as many drops as needed to fill your pet's ear canal with the ear cleaning liquid daily. The daily  must be continued for a period of no less than 7 days, depending on the severity of the build-up in your pet's ears. (Be cautious to watch your pet's ears closely during the  as we have found some pet's will have some slight irritation around day 5-7, so use your judgment and discontinue daily drops if needed.) Do not clean your pets ears out during the primary phase, simply insert the drops daily. Only clean the area outside of the ear canal as the product begins to pull the debris clear of the inner ear. After the primary phase, clean your pet’s ears thoroughly using a cotton pad or cotton swab wet with product; (NEVER USE A Q-TIP IN YOUR PETS EARS!) Check your pet's ears again in 3 days, if all debris is still gone you can continue with the maintenance phase. If after 3 days more debris has built up, you will need to continue with daily application for an additional week, and then recheck. MAINTENANCE PHASE: Once your pet's chronic build-up is gone you are in maintenance phase. To maintain future good ear health, use product once every 1-2 weeks as needed, and clean debris as needed after application. Safe and effective for pets with or without fur. Only caution is if your pet has excessive ear hair like in poodle breeds, hair must be removed prior to use of product. Ingredients: organic witch hazel, organic vegetable glycerin colloidal silver, organic aloe vera, fractionated coconut oil, non-gmo vitamin e., proprietary blend of oil extracts. ***please note our formulations are proprietary to protect our brand. Nail and paw debris is often caused by a combination of dirt, litter, dust, and even chronic over-growth of yeast. Many of these chronic yeast over-growths however, go highly un-diagnosed. ReNewedPet® nail/paw cleaner is designed to not only remove unwanted debris, but to arrest the cause of the build-up so it does not return after a few days like with other products. Suitable for all pets with or without fur. DIRECTIONS FOR USE: PRIMARY PHASE: The primary phase helps to reduce the initial build-up of debris which may be caused by a chronic yeast infection. In this phase, use a cotton pad and apply small amounts of cleaner onto both nails and nailbeds; allow product to sit on nails for a minimum of one minute. Next, use old toothbrush or nail brush to gently brush the nails to further loosen the debris. Lastly, using a clean cotton pad continue soaked again in product, continue to remove all debris. It is very important that this be done daily, or the product will not work as intended. Three days after the primary phase is complete, check your pet’s nails. If all debris has not returned, you can continue with the maintenance phase. If after three days, debris has built up, continue with daily application for another period of 1 week and then recheck. MAINTENANCE PHASE: Once you have completed the initial primary phase and all debris is cleared, you are in maintenance phase. To maintain future good nail/paw health, clean your pet’s nails once every 1-2 weeks as needed. *Be certain to use daily in the Primary Phase. Ingredients: organic witch hazel, organic vegetable glycerin, colloidal silver, organic shea butter, fractionated coconut oil, organic aloe vera oil, non-gmo vitamin e. oil, tapioca starch, proprietary blend of herbal extracts. ***please note our formulations are proprietary to protect our brand. Catnip contains the chemical "nepetalactones" which is what cats react to in the plant and create the altered mood. In the silver vine plant, the reactive compound is called "nepetalacol" which some cats react to more than that of catnip creating a more intense affect. This is why the combination of catnip and silver vine is a premium product, because for cats who would not otherwise react to catnip, will often have a great response form the silver vine, meaning no kitty goes without FUN! WHY CHOOSE FARM TO PET DEER ANTLER DOG CHEWS Farm to Pet Deer Antlers for Dogs are the best dog chew for large dogs with a need to gnaw! These safe natural dog chews cater to a dog's instinctual urge to chew without the risks of bones or dog chew toys, providing a healthy outlet for energy with a tasty yet nutritious reward. In addition, Farm to Pet offers only premium grade antlers, selected for quality and harvested by hand after being harmlessly shed and honed to chewable paw-fection! DEER ANTLER DOG CHEW INGREDIENT SOURCE Wild-gathered in Illinois and Wisconsin USA HOW TO CHOOSE AN ANTLER DOG CHEW Before giving your dog an antler chew, here are useful tips to determine what type, style and size of antler chew is best suited for your dog's size and chewing style. Deer Antlers for Dogs Deer antler chews are our hardest and largest chews. These whole antlers are best suited for very aggressive and experienced chewers. Farm to Pet Deer Antlers are available in L and XL sizes only for dogs 35 lbs and higher. Reindeer Antlers for Dogs Relndeer antler dog chews are also suited for aggressive chewers but come in more sizes and whole and split versions. Whole Reindeer Antler Chews are very tough and require aggressive chewing to reach the marrow. Split Reindeer Antler Chews are also tough, but come with marrow already exposed. Farm to Pet Reindeer Antlers are available in S (for dogs 1-15 lbs), M (for dogs 15-35 lbs) and L (for dogs 35 lbs and higher). Elk Antlers for Dogs Elk antler chews are suited for a range of dog sizes, as well as chewers from beginner to aggressive. Whole Elk Antlers still require aggressive chewing to reach the marrow, but the antlers are slightly less tough than deer and reindeer antlers. Split Elk Antlers are the best for less aggressive chewers or those introducing antler chews to their dogs. Farm to Pet Elk Antlers are available in S (for dogs 1-15 lbs), M (for dogs 15-35 lbs), L and Giant (for dogs 35 lbs and higher). DOG ANTLER CHEW SIZE CHART The following table summarizes our antler chews versus the size of your dog. Whole/Split Small 1-15 LBS Whole/Split Medium 15-35 LBS Whole/Split Large 35+ LBS Whole Giant/Extra Large 35+ LBS FARM TO PET ANTLER DOG CHEW SAFETY GUIDELINES Never choose a small antler just to try it out. It may become a choking hazard. Always choose an antler dog chew in proportion to dog size. They should be able to hold antlers in their paws and chew on one end. Supervise dogs when they are chewing an antler chew, especially aggressive chewers. Regularly inspect the antler chews and replace if there are signs of excessive wear, breakage or splintering. Discard an antler chew before it reaches a size that can become a choking hazard. Puppies should not be given antler chews until their milk teeth have fallen out, usually after six months of age. Antler chews should not be given to dogs with broken or missing teeth or other dental issues. Consult your vet with any safety or health concerns. HOW TO USE ANTLER CHEWS FOR DOGS So many uses, so much time! Here are a few ways to incorporate organic antler chews into your dog's daily life. Chew Time: Antler dog chews are ideal to satisfy your pup's natural instinct to chew, providing mental stimulation and physical exertion as well as nutritional and dental benefits. Exercise: Not only is chewing exercise in itself, you can encourage physical activity by incorporating antler chews into interactive play sessions with your dog. Anxiety Remedy: Antlers are great dog calming chews that can help alleviate stress and anxiety. Boredom Buster: Antler dog chews are a great way to keep dogs entertained, prevent boredom and provide a sense of accomplishment. Training Reward: Use antler chews as a high-value reward during training sessions to reinforce positive behavior and encourage learning. Distraction: An antler chew can keep dogs occupied and distracted during stressful situations, such as thunderstorms or fireworks. Socialization: Introduce antler chews during socialization sessions with other dogs to promote positive interactions and play. ANTLER DOG CHEW FAQS ARE ANTLERS SAFE FOR DOGS TO CHEW? Farm to Pet antler chews are healthy and safe chews for dogs. Unlike bones, our organic antler sheds for dogs are naturally splinter-resistant, long-lasting and durable, able to withstand even aggressive chewing by powerful canine jaws. Keep in mind that dogs should not be given any dog chews including antler dog chews if they have weak, loose or broken teeth or to puppies who still have their milk teeth. Dogs should be supervised any time they are enjoying chew time with their favorite chew toy, including antler dog chews. WHAT IS THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN ELK, REINDEER AND DEER ANTLERS FOR DOGS? While all antlers make tough dog chews, Elk, Deer and Reindeer Antlers for dogs vary slightly in toughness and durability. Deer antlers are slightly tougher than elk antlers. Reindeer antlers are tougher than both elk and deer antlers: Elk antler chews = tough Deer antler chews = tougher Reindeer antler chews = toughest WHAT IS THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN WHOLE AND SPLIT ANTLER CHEWS? Whole antler sheds for dogs are intact antlers that have been cut at the ends to create different lengths that are appropriate for various dog sizes, then smoothed and honed to be safe for chewing. Split antlers for dogs are whole antlers that have been literally split in half lengthwise to expose the marrow in the middle. Spilt antlers of any type are long-lasting dog chews but slightly less durable than whole versions of the same antler type. Since the marrow is exposed, split antlers make a better choice for beginners or chewers with shorter attention spans. Whole antler chews are better suited and may last longer for experienced and aggressive chewers. ARE ANTLERS DOG CHEWS HEALTHY FOR DOGS? Absolutely! Farm to Pet organic antler chews are rich in the following nutrients that support overall canine wellness: Calcium Phosphorus Magnesium Potassium Zinc Glucosamine and chondroitin sulfate In addition, antler dog chews promote strong jaws and good dental hygiene by helping to reduce plaque and tartar build up. Antler chews are also a non-allergenic, low-fat and low-calorie source of protein and amino acids for dogs. MY DOG CAN’T CHEW. HOW CAN I GET THE NUTRIENTS OF ANTLERS WITHOUT THE CHEWING? Even for dogs who are chewing challenged - whether seniors with missing choppers, puppies with milk teeth, or the rare pooch who simply doesn’t like to chew - they can get all the nutritional benefits of antler chews in powder form! Thanks to Farm to Pet Treat Topper Antler Powder dog food topper, you can sprinkle on the same nutrients and flavor on wet food, dry food, or lick mat treat anytime - no chewing required!

Pet hoodies are a great way to keep your pet warm, while also managing shedding, dirt, ticks, and more! They provide a fun way to keep your pet cleaner and happier! All of our hoodies are soft and comfy, double stitched in all the right places to ensure durability! The material content is 65% cotton, 35% polyester - the best mix for long lasting wear and tear! Please be sure to use our sizing chart (located in the additional pictures, underneath the main image), our sizing is much smaller than some brands to better fit the little (and big!) bodies we fit. Due to concerns with hygiene, we cannot take returns, but we will make it right if your hoodie doesn't fit! WHAT MAKES FARM TO PET FISH DOG TREATS SPECIAL? As a rule, dogs can usually enjoy 10-20 percent of their daily calories in treats. However, many of us don’t know what our dog’s daily calorie target is or how many calories they take in! Luckily, you can base how many treats to give your dog on your dog’s size. Our grain-free fish dog treats have eight calories per chip. This means your small pup can have from 2-4 fish chips for dogs per day; medium dogs can eat 5-7 chips, and large dogs can enjoy up to 10 chips per day.
